## Poland events by Matoro ##

add_namespace = poland
add_namespace = polandflavor
add_namespace = polandnews

### Starting Events ###
country_event = { #Intro
	id = poland.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.0" }
	title = poland.0.t
	desc = poland.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_regency_stamp

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.0.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		country_event = poland.1
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.0.b
	}
}

country_event = { #Future of the Privy Council
	id = poland.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.6" }
	title = poland.6.t
	desc = poland.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_royal_castle

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			POL_august_iv = {
				remove_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
				remove_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				remove_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_geheimrat1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL_august_iv = {
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat1 ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat1 ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat1 ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.6.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_geheimrat2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL_august_iv = {
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat2 ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat2 ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat2 ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.6.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_geheimrat3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL_august_iv = {
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat3 ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat3 ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
				add_trait = { trait = POL_geheimrat3 ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #PPS's leadership
	id = poland.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.7" }
	title = poland.7.t
	desc = poland.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_PPS

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.7.a #Barlicki
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois
				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -5 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki }
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland.7.barlicki_tt2
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland.7.barlicki_tt1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland.114
			FRA = { country_event = poland.114 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland.114 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.7.b #Dubois
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				has_country_flag = POL_AUS_supported_barlicki
				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -10 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois
		clr_country_flag = POL_PPS_Barlicki
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_FRA_supported_dubois }
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland.7.dubois_tt2
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = poland.7.dubois_tt1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland.114
			FRA = { country_event = poland.114 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland.114 }
		}
	}
}

		name = poland.8.b

	}
}

country_event = { #Peasant unrest (prelude to the strike)
	id = poland.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.9" }
	title = poland.9.t
	desc = poland.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_peasant_revolt

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland.10 days = 46 } #Peasant strikes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois } }
				country_event = { id = poland.11 days = 52 } #PPS joins if pro-Rep
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = poland.13 days = 12 } } #inform GER
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.9.a
		add_stability = -0.04
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.9.b
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -4 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
	}
}

}

		}

		}

		name = poland.11.b

			days = 60
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}

		}

##Underground events
country_event = { #Republicans smuggling from Galicia
	id = poland.22
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.22" }
	title = poland.22.t
	desc = poland.22.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owns_state = 88 }
		POL_has_monarchy = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.22.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_talks_with_galicia }
			GAL = { exists = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
				is_ai = no
			}
			country_event = poland.31
		}
		else = {
			GAL = { country_event = poland.31 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 4 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = POL_talks_with_galicia
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.22.b
		add_political_power = -25
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 4 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}

country_event = {
	id = poland.81
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event polandfla.12" }
	title = poland.81.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_major_purge }
		text = poland.81.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_minor_purge }
		text = poland.81.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_no_purge }
		text = poland.81.d3
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = POL_krakow_conspiracy
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 6
					has_country_flag = POL_army_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_bund_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_unions_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_church_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PPS
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PSL
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_chjena
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_major_purge
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					has_country_flag = POL_army_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_bund_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_unions_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_church_investigated
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PPS
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_PSL
					has_country_flag = POL_investigated_chjena
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_minor_purge
		}
		else = { set_country_flag = POL_no_purge }
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.81.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_major_purge }
			clr_country_flag = POL_major_purge
			add_ideas = POL_decimated_underground
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_minor_purge }
			clr_country_flag = POL_minor_purge
			add_ideas = POL_weakened_underground
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = POL_no_purge
				if = {
					limit = {
						POL = { is_ai = yes }
					}
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_NO_REVOLT } }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = POL_no_purge
			add_ideas = POL_active_underground
		}
	}
}

			}

				NOT = {

					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }

					}

			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -7 }
			POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_nat_reduce_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_fraud_PSL }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -7 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_rep_reduce_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_fraud_circle }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -7 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.119.b
	}
}

country_event = { #Elections of 1938
	id = poland.150
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.150" }
	title = poland.150.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_sejm

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_MARLIB }
			}
			set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 45 }
			set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 25 }
			set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 15 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
			}
			set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 20 }
			set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 20 }
			set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 45 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
			}
			set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 45 }
			set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 20 }
			set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 20 }
			set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 15 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_idea = POL_coalition_broken } }
					add_ideas = POL_coalition_broken
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCDEM_GER }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 45 }
			set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
			set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 45 }
			set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { is_ai = yes }
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_REP_SOCCON_GER }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				10 = {
					set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
					set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 45 }
					set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 15 }
					set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
				}
				10 = {
					set_variable = { POL_royal_influence = 15 }
					set_variable = { POL_soc_influence = 15 }
					set_variable = { POL_rep_influence = 45 }
					set_variable = { POL_nat_influence = 25 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.circle_coalition
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_circle_victory > 50 }
			NOT = { has_idea = POL_coalition_broken }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.circle
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 50 } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.chjena_coalition
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_circle_victory > 50 }
			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence > POL_royal_influence }
			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence < 50 }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.chjena
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence > 50 }
			NOT = { has_idea = POL_coalition_broken }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.chjena_coalition_broken
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence > 50 }
			has_idea = POL_coalition_broken
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.centrolew
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_centrolew_victory > 50 } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.150.d.stalemate
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_royal_influence < 50 }
			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence < 50 }

	is_triggered_only = yes

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_circle_victory > POL_centrolew_victory } }
			set_country_flag = POL_circle_real_victory
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois }
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_rep_real_victory
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { POL_centrolew_victory > POL_circle_victory }

				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Barlicki }
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_soc_real_victory
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.150.a #Current government wins
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_circle_victory > POL_centrolew_victory }

		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland.151 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = poland.155 days = 7 }
			news_event = { id = worldnews.486 days = 1 }
		}

		set_politics = {

		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.150.b #Circle majority
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 50 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland.151 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = poland.155 days = 7 }
			news_event = { id = worldnews.486 days = 1 }
		}

			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.2 }
	}

			check_variable = { POL_nat_influence > POL_royal_influence }

		}

		hidden_effect = {

		}

			elections_allowed = yes
		}

		add_to_coalition = yes

		activate_advisor = POL_jozef_chacinski_sic
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.025 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.025 }

#The King Appoints Studnicki
country_event = {
	id = poland.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.152" }
	title = poland.152.t
	desc = poland.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_studnicki

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = POL_coalition_broken
			remove_ideas = POL_sejm_dismissed
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.152.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_circle_real_victory } }
			add_political_power = -50
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = -20 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		remove_from_coalition = yes

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}

		clear_sic_slot = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_wladyslaw_studnicki_sic
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		complete_national_focus = POL_Election_of_1938
		clr_country_flag = POL_supported_jews
	}
}

country_event = { #Elections of 1942
	id = poland.153
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.153" }
	title = poland.153.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = market_liberal
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		text = poland.153.d.free
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		text = poland.153.d.auth
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_sejm

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1939.01.01
		POL_has_monarchy = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_second_monarchy_election }
	}
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = POL_second_monarchy_election
		end_coalition = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.153.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 40 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 50 } }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 5 }
		}
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		}
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.08
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.153.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_AUTDEM }
					has_completed_focus = POL_Entrenched_Constitutionalism
					has_completed_focus = POL_Constitutionalist_Coalition
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_royal_influence > 50 } }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 5 }
		}
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		}
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_nat_reduce_tt

			hold_election = ROOT

			activate_mission = POL_centrolew_reform_mission
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.204.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_election_barlicki }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }

				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 36
			elections_allowed = yes
		}

			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_ideas = POL_republic_instability1
		set_country_flag = POL_first_republican_election
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_malinowski
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_barlicki
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_dubois

				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_AUS }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_election option = POL_ELECTION_SOCLIB_GER }
				}
			}
		}

			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 36
			elections_allowed = yes

		clear_sic_slot = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_stanislaw_dubois_sic

			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}

			popularity = 0.02

		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_ideas = POL_republic_instability1
		set_country_flag = POL_first_republican_election
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_malinowski
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_barlicki
		clr_country_flag = POL_election_dubois
	}

country_event = { #Republic of Poland re-joins Reichspakt
	id = poland.225
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.225" }
	title = poland.225.t
	desc = poland.225.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.225.a
		get_current_government_type = yes
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = POL
			set_autonomy = {
				target = POL
				autonomy_state = kr_oststaat
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
			add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
			clr_country_flag = POL_forpol_wait
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 5 }
		POL_add_german_influence = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_trade_finished }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_polish_control }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_polish_control
					add_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
					add_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
					add_idea = POL_german_hegemony
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
					add_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = POL_german_hegemony
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
			POL_add_german_influence = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
		##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_soc_tt
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
		##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_nat_tt
	}
}

#Polish Galicia agrees to join
country_event = {
	id = poland.235
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.235" }
	title = poland.235.t
	desc = poland.235.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#country_event = { id = polandflavor.20 months = 20 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.235.a
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		GAL_characters_join_poland_immediate = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = polandflavor.29 days = 365 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland.236 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_former_faction_member }
				}
				GER = { country_event = poland.237 }
			}
			POL_transfer_popularity = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.25
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GAL = { exists = yes } }
				GAL = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = POL
						size = 0.6
						stockpile_ratio = 0.6
						army_ratio = 0.6
						air_ratio = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		88 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_GAL_characters
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_polish_control }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_polish_control
				add_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_austrian_friendship
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				add_idea = POL_austrian_cooperation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austrian_friendship }
			88 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			91 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = { add_ideas = POL_austrian_cooperation }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { POL_has_monarchy = no }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 35 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 20 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		AUS = { country_event = poland.246 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = GER
				GER = { has_elected_government = yes }
			}
			effect_tooltip = { GER = { end_puppet = POL } }
		}
	}
}

	}

country_event = {
	id = poland.245
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.245" }
	title = poland.245.t
	desc = poland.245.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_rydz

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_socialist_government = no }
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.245.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = POL
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			GER = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = topple_government
					target = POL
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.245.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #The Issue of Lemberg
	id = poland.246
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.246" }
	title = poland.246.t
	desc = poland.246.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Divide it, but give Lwów to the Poles; happens if poles are allies but ukr isn't that bad either
		name = poland.246.a
		trigger = {
			UKR = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				POL = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
						has_left_democratic_government = yes
					}
				}
				UKR = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUS
						has_left_democratic_government = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.250 } #union with lwow
		UKR = {
			set_country_flag = POL_UKR_partition
			country_event = poland.248
		}

	}
	option = { #Everything for Ukraine
		name = poland.246.b
		trigger = {
			UKR = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				UKR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					NOT = { has_government = social_conservative } #no annexation for Russia
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
				POL = { POL_evil_monarchy = yes }
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			set_country_flag = POL_UKR_everything
			country_event = poland.248
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.249 } #Austria keeps it
	}
	option = { #Everything for Poland
		name = poland.246.c
		trigger = {
			POL = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				POL = {
					is_in_faction_with = AUS
					has_left_democratic_government = yes
				}
				UKR = {
					has_left_democratic_government = no
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.247 } #union with eastern galicia
	}
	option = { #keep it; if both are bad choices
		name = poland.246.f
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				POL = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				UKR = {
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AUS }
					has_left_democratic_government = no
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.249 } #Austria keeps it
		if = {
			limit = { GAL = { exists = yes } }
			AUS = {
				annex_country = {
					target = GAL
					transfer_troops = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = GAL
						}
						add_core_of = AUS
						remove_core_of = GAL
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Autonomous Territory of Eastern Galicia
	id = poland.247
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.247" }
	title = poland.247.t
	desc = poland.247.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.247.a
		trigger = { tag = POL }
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		88 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
		91 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		89 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					GAL = {
						controls_state = 80
						controls_state = 713
					}
					AUS = {
						controls_state = 80
						controls_state = 713
					}
				}
			}
			80 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
			713 = { transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = POL }
			}
			add_compliance = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GAL = { owns_state = 73 } #Transcarpathia
			}
			var:664.owner = { country_event = poland.258 } #Owner of Southern Slovakia
		}
	}
}

			}

		trigger = { NOT = { owns_state = 91 } }
		text = poland.251.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { owns_state = 91 }
		text = poland.251.d2
	}
	trigger = { owns_state = 1088 }
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.251.a
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 3 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { POL_rep_influence > 10 } }
				country_event = { id = poland.252 days = 14 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 91 }
				country_event = { id = poland.253 days = 210 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Coup Plan (Parasol)
country_event = {
	id = poland.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.255" }
	title = poland.255.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland.255.d.monarchy
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = no }
		text = poland.255.d.republic
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_rydz

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.255.a
		if = {
			limit = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
			POL_return_purged_generals = yes
			clear_army_chief = yes
			activate_advisor = POL_edward_rydz_smigly_army_chief
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_unable_to_remove_tt
		}
		else = {
			add_war_support = 0.04
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = POL_operation_parasol }
		}
	}
}

	desc = poland.261.d

			surrender_progress > 0.9

				controls_state = 777
			}
		}
		POL = {
			has_left_democratic_government = yes

		name = poland.261.a

	}
	option = {
		name = poland.261.b

		add_state_claim = 67

		add_state_claim = 777

	}
}

country_event = { #Subsequent republic presidential election
	id = poland.270
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.270" }
	title = poland.270.t
	desc = poland.270.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_presidency

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = poland.270 days = 1460 } #Presidential elections every 4th year
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.270.a
		trigger = { POL_norbert_barlicki = { is_second_in_command = no } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_norbert_barlicki
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_norbert_barlicki
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.270.b
		trigger = { owns_state = 67 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_stanislaw_mikolajczyk
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_stanislaw_mikolajczyk
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.270.c
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
			promote_character = {
				character = POL_jan_woznicki
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
		}
		else = {

#Demands
country_event = {
	id = poland.275
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.275" }
	title = poland.275.t
	desc = {
		text = poland.275.d.fra
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.275.d.rus
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.275.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations }
		country_event = { id = poland.278 days = 14 }
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = polandnews.1 days = 15 }
		}
		remove_ideas = {
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_1
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_2
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_3
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_1
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_2
			POL_dawn_of_progress_psl_3
			POL_dawn_of_progress_pps_psl_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			leave_faction = yes
			POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
			POL_remove_guderian = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = ROOT }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
		}
		FRA = { add_to_faction = POL }
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { country_event = poland.276 }
			clr_country_flag = POL_INT_negotiations
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.275.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations }
		country_event = { id = poland.279 days = 14 }
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = polandnews.2 days = 15 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			leave_faction = yes
			POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
			POL_remove_guderian = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = ROOT }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		RUS = { add_to_faction = POL }
		hidden_effect = {
			INT = { country_event = poland.276 }
			clr_country_flag = POL_RUS_negotiations
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.275.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = poland.277 }
	}
}

#Poland gives in to the French
country_event = {
	id = poland.278
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.278" }
	title = poland.278.t
	desc = poland.278.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_revolution

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.278.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_WK2_reparations }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_WK2_reparations_fra
				days = 730
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = POL_Revolutionary_Republic
		if = {
			limit = { INT = { has_government = totalist } }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			clear_sic_slot = yes
			activate_advisor = POL_stanislaw_bukowiecki_sic
		}
		else = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = syndicalist
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			clear_sic_slot = yes
			activate_advisor = POL_pawel_lew_marek_sic
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = totalist }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:totalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_stability = -0.15
		POL_purge_right_generals = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			POL_konstanty_rokossowski = { set_nationality = POL }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = { POL_konstanty_rokossowski = { set_nationality = POL } }
		}
	}
}

			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_rep_reduce_tt
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = {#Economic treaty between POL, GER and AUS
	id = poland.313
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.313" }
	title = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland.313.t.pol
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } }
		text = poland.313.t.ger
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland.313.d.pol
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } }
		text = poland.313.d.ger
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control0
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control1
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control2
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control3
			remove_ideas = POL_german_control4
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets0
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets1
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets2
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets3
			remove_ideas = POL_austrian_assets4
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.313.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }#poles control their economy
		add_ideas = POL_polish_control
		add_political_power = POL_influence
		set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 10 }
		POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = poland.314 }
			AUS = { country_event = poland.314 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.313.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 50 } } #poles don't control
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { POL_GER_influence > 30 }
				check_variable = { POL_AUS_influence < 10 }
				GER = { exists = yes }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_german_cooperation
			set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 3 }
			POL_add_syndicalist_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_soc_tt
			POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_nat_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { POL_AUS_influence > 30 }
				check_variable = { POL_GER_influence < 10 }
				AUS = { exists = yes }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_austrian_cooperation
			set_temp_variable = { POL.POL_influence_change = 5 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
			##custom_effect_tooltip = POL_rep_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { AUS = { exists = yes } }
			add_ideas = POL_austro_german_condominium
		}
		else = { add_ideas = POL_german_cooperation }
	}
}

#Germany fulfills the promises
country_event = {
	id = poland.328
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.328" }
	title = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_independence }
		text = poland.328.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_autonomy }
		text = poland.328.t2
	}
	desc = poland.328.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.328.a
		get_current_government_type = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_autonomy }
			GER = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = POL
					autonomy_state = kr_oststaat_autonomous
					end_wars = no
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = POL_autonomy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_independence }
			GER = { end_puppet = POL }
			clr_country_flag = POL_independence
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		if = { #Fix accidental removal of the cosmetic tag
			limit = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom } }
			set_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 10 }
		if = {
			limit = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_left_democratic_government = yes }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}
		add_stability = 0.15
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_hegemony }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_hegemony
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_german_cooperation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_german_cooperation
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_austro_german_condominium
				add_idea = POL_polish_control
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = poland.334

	desc = poland.334.d

			}

				name = poland.334.t

				}
			}

country_event = { #Germany decreases recruitment in Poland
	id = poland.352
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.352" }
	title = poland.352.t
	desc = poland.352.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_factory_workers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.352.a
		if = {
			limit = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 3 }
			POL_add_royal_influence = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 3 }
			POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_recruitment }
			remove_ideas = POL_recruitment
			effect_tooltip = {
				GER = { remove_ideas = POL_GER_recruitment }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = POL_recruitment_2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = POL_recruitment_2
				add_idea = POL_recruitment
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				GER = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = POL_GER_recruitment_2
						add_idea = POL_GER_recruitment
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 8 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = POL_moderate_land_reform
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		80 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = POL }
		713 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = POL }
		owns_state = 79
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			AUS = { is_subject = yes }
			AUS = { exists = no }
			owns_state = 84 #Transylvania
			is_in_faction_with = AUS
			is_puppet_of = AUS
			POL = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AUS } } #POL not in DA doesn't care about Austria's opinion
			is_puppet_of = POL
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.490.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		POL = {
			country_event = { id = poland.491 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.490.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -20
	}
}

	}

#Nationalist coup
country_event = {
	id = poland.411
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.411" }
	title = poland.411.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland.411.d.kingdom
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = no }
		text = poland.411.d.republic
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BUL_Zveno_Coup

	immediate = {
		POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.411.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland.419
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		clear_sic_slot = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_tadeusz_bielecki_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		POL_set_up_uprising = yes
		activate_mission = POL_military_takeover
		activate_mission = POL_sejm_revolt
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = polandnews.6
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_PATAUT }
					paternal_autocrat < 0.1
					POL = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.1
				}
			}
			POL_update_military = yes
		}
	}
}

#The Strike turns into Revolution
country_event = {
	id = poland.413
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.413" }
	title = poland.413.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
		text = poland.413.d.kingdom
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { POL_has_monarchy = no }
		text = poland.413.d.republic
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_revolution

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = POL_socialist_uprising
		POL_overthrow_monarchy = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.413.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = poland.418
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.1
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = polandnews.5
		}
		clear_sic_slot = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_pawel_lew_marek_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:totalist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = POL_PPS_Dubois }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			POL_konstanty_rokossowski = { set_nationality = POL }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = { POL_konstanty_rokossowski = { set_nationality = POL } }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = POL_totalist2_party_long
				name = POL_totalist2_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = POL_syndicalist3_party_long
				name = POL_syndicalist3_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = POL_radical_socialist3_party_long
				name = POL_radical_socialist3_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = POL_social_democrat3_party_long
				name = POL_social_democrat3_party
			}
			POL_update_military = yes
		}
		POL_set_up_uprising = yes
	}
}

#Warning event
country_event = {
	id = poland.420
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.420" }
	title = poland.420.t
	desc = poland.420.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			POL = { POL_syndicalist_revolution_trigger = yes }
			POL = { POL_nationalist_uprising_trigger = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.420.a
		setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { POL_syndicalist_revolution_trigger = yes } }
			set_country_flag = POL_revolt_warning_syndicalist
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { POL = { POL_nationalist_uprising_trigger = yes } }
			set_country_flag = POL_revolt_warning_nationalist
		}
	}
}

#Massive Economic Crash
country_event = {
	id = poland.561
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.561" }
	title = poland.561.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence < 51 } }
		text = poland.561.d.a
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 50 } }
		text = poland.561.d.b
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday
	trigger = { NOT = { has_idea = POL_polish_control } }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = POL_uprising_crash
			if = { limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = POL_economic_restructuring_2 }
			}
			else = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = POL_economic_restructuring_1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.561.a
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash1
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.561.b
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash3
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.561.c
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { POL_influence > 51 } }
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash5
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = POL_uprising_crash6
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = poland.604

	title = poland.604.t
	desc = poland.604.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_council

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.604.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_SYNDIE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader_with_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution } }
			add_country_leader_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = POL_kazimierz_zakrzewski
			ideology = totalist_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			long_name = POL_syndicalist3_party_long
			name = POL_syndicalist3_party
		}
		clear_sic_slot = yes
		activate_advisor = POL_stanislaw_bukowiecki_sic
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = poland.606 }
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.604.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_revolts option = POL_REVOLTS_TOTALIST }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution }
			remove_country_leader_trait = POL_dictator_of_revolution
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = { id = poland.607 days = 7 }
	}
}

#Governing the Eastern Regions
country_event = {
	id = poland.650
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.650" }
	title = poland.650.t
	desc = poland.650.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.650.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 202 #Kiev
				owns_state = 206 #Minsk
				check_variable = { num_owned_states > 40 }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 202
				owns_state = 206
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 202
					owns_state = 206
				}
			}
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_2
		}
		else = { #only Lithuania
			add_ideas = POL_eastern_governments_1
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		country_event = poland.651
		hidden_effect = { news_event = polandnews.8 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Death of Dowbor-Musnicki
	id = polandflavor.26
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event polandfla.26" }
	title = polandflavor.26.t
	desc = polandflavor.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_funeral

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = polandflavor.26.a
		retire_character = POL_jozef_dowbor_musnicki
		POL_leon_berbecki = {
			promote_leader = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = polandflavor.26.b
		trigger = { has_character = POL_kazimierz_sosnkowski }
		retire_character = POL_jozef_dowbor_musnicki
		POL_kazimierz_sosnkowski = {
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 3 }
		POL_add_republican_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = polandflavor.26.c
		retire_character = POL_jozef_dowbor_musnicki
		POL_jozef_haller_von_hallenburg = {
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { POL_influence_change = 3 }
		POL_add_nationalist_influence = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = polandflavor.26.e
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		retire_character = POL_jozef_dowbor_musnicki
		hidden_effect = { add_command_power = 50 }
	}
}

country_event = { #debug event to log the path that Poland is on at 1.1.1939
	id = poland.999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event poland.999" }
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = KR.hidden.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND HAS MARKET LIBERAL GOVERNMENT;[GetDateText];[ROOT.GetName];[FROM.GetName]"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND HAS AUTHORITARIAN DEMOCRAT GOVERNMENT;[GetDateText];[ROOT.GetName];[FROM.GetName]"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative }
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND HAS SOCIAL CONSERVATIVE GOVERNMENT;[GetDateText];[ROOT.GetName];[FROM.GetName]"
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;POLAND HAS SOCIAL LIBERAL OR SOCIAL DEMOCRAT GOVERNMENT;[GetDateText];[ROOT.GetName];[FROM.GetName]"
		}
	}
}

### World News Events ###

news_event = { #Poland-Internationale Peace
	id = polandnews.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event polandnews.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = polandnews.1.t
	desc = polandnews.1.d
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = RUS } }
		text = polandnews.1.d.norussia
	}
	picture = GFX_news_event_POL_syndicalism

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.1.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = RUS
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = polandnews.1.a.russia
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = polandnews.1.a.socialist
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #Rydz Coup
	id = polandnews.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event polandnews.2 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = polandnews.4.t
	desc = {
		text = polandnews.4.d.centrolew_ultimatum
		trigger = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = polandnews.4.d.centrolew_accept
		trigger = {
			POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt }
			POL = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = polandnews.4.d.parasol
		trigger = { NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt } } }
	}
	picture = GFX_news_event_POL_military_takeover

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	trigger = { wants_world_news = yes }

	show_major = { regional_europe_news = yes }

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.a
		trigger = {
			tag = POL
			OR = {
				POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz }
				NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			OR = {
				POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz }
				NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = POL }
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			OR = {
				POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz }
				NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.e
		trigger = {
			tag = POL
			NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
			POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = POL }
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
			POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.4.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			NOT = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_ultimatum_against_rydz } }
			POL = { has_country_flag = POL_rydz_coup_attempt }
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.9.c #For Germany
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}

	option = {
		name = polandnews.9.e #For everyone else
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = GER }
			NOT = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			NOT = { has_left_democratic_government = yes }
		}
	}
}
